      "source": [
        "### 2주차에 배운 문법들은 -> 행과 열 기준 인덱스 기준으로 데이터를 찾아가는 것, 추출하는 경우\n",
        "### 3주차에 배우는 문법은 -> 데이터 분석에 필요한 문법 -> 데이터를 추출하기위한 조건의 문버\n",
        "- 아래 문법들은 내가 원하는 요구조건의 데이터를 추출할 때 사용할 수 있는 문법"
      ]
    },

      },
      "source": [
        "## 데이터 분석에 필요한 분석 기초 문법\n",
        "- query() - 데이터의 조건에 따른 추출\n",
        "- 행,열 추출 loc,iloc [], [[]] (2주차에 진행)\n",
        "    - df[[불린값]] - 불린값 형태의 데이터 추출\n",
        "- sort_values() -정렬\n",
        "- 파생변수 만들기\n",
        "- assign(), lambda,\n",
        "- groupby()와 함께 사용하는 agg() -데이터를 집계함수\n",
        "- merge(), concat() - 데이터 병합\n",
        "- str() - 문자열 데이터를 다룰 때\n",
        "- 시계열 - 시계열 데이터를 다룰 때 사용"
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",

              "    <script>\n",
              "      const buttonEl =\n",
              "        document.querySelector('#df-5c04d863-5f1a-4c1b-81a1-77b3aff66338 button.colab-df-convert');\n",
              "      buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "        google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-5c04d863-5f1a-4c1b-81a1-77b3aff66338');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "\n",

              "\n",
              "  <script>\n",
              "    async function quickchart(key) {\n",

        "# Query()\n",
        "- 쿼리 -> 내가 원하는 데이터의 조건을 질의한다.\n",
        "- 그 조건을 명확하게 어떤 식으로 작성해야 하는지? 문법적인 부분을 이해하고 데이터를 추출하자!\n",
        "- 데이터프레임의 문법\n",
        "- 데이터프레임.query('조건')\n",
        "\n",
        "- 데이터프레임에 작동하는 문법"
      ]

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-41b2c299-1a7d-44a5-b33c-7119548b62d2');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-90b9b52d-f150-4d7f-a31f-19a66e22e4bb');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-52ec9141-64e2-4c5a-9b74-bbf161cf5c44');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-3f99f9ab-fc7d-43d0-ab33-3a6abf69c9bf');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",

              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",

              "        document.querySelector('#df-4cff675b-feee-43a8-85fb-70dc78bdbc13 button.colab-df-convert');\n",
              "      buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "        google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-4cff675b-feee-43a8-85fb-70dc78bdbc13');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "\n",
              "\n",
              "<div id=\"df-4994f559-8da3-4929-b0be-442b43ecab93\">\n",

              "            title=\"Suggest charts\"\n",
              "            style=\"display:none;\">\n",
              "\n",
              "<svg xmlns=\"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\" height=\"24px\"viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\"\n",

              "\n",
              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-08166a95-f115-4d14-9dd4-dfc8721f32d4');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",

              "      quickchartButtonEl.disabled = true;  // To prevent multiple clicks.\n",
              "      quickchartButtonEl.classList.add('colab-df-spinner');\n",
              "      try {\n",

              "            'suggestCharts', [key], {});\n",
              "      } catch (error) {\n",
              "        console.error('Error during call to suggestCharts:', error);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "      quickchartButtonEl.classList.remove('colab-df-spinner');\n",
              "      quickchartButtonEl.classList.add('colab-df-quickchart-complete');\n",

              "      buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "        google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-18466758-0fe3-498d-9fc4-4fb75555411e');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",

              "      quickchartButtonEl.classList.add('colab-df-quickchart-complete');\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-414fa0c6-762c-4226-b0ef-8fac13664921');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-a3be3404-ae29-41df-af17-dc7699bfeb3a');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",

              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",

              "      }\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",

              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",

              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-b136b2d3-4cdd-48c2-ad44-a9db841398de');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-6f7e5e69-0238-4e0d-8eff-7663de5d463b');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-606fc5e4-7caa-4080-99cf-0977c6d016e7');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-5107c761-a005-4b26-8231-67ab4d244f05');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-9f97f262-6f35-4bdf-be47-38278eb59285');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",

              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",

              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-0efc220e-c152-407a-8c34-f88d67a2ca11');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",

              "      buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "        google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "      async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "        const element = document.querySelector('#df-f3c1eb5a-f6d1-4c5e-b892-830704bf5ed9');\n",
              "        const dataTable =\n",
              "          await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                    [key], {});\n",
              "        if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "        const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "          '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "          + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "        element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "        dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "        await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "        const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "        docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "        element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "      }\n",
              "    </script>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "\n",

      "source": [
        "## 필수과제들\n",
        "- **필수과제1**\n",
        "-  q1 - pclass 3 이고, age 20세 미만인 남성과, 여성의 카운트 수와 생존수를 비교해 주세요.\n",
        "    - 코드와 데이터 값\n",
        "\n",
        "- **필수과제2**\n",
        "- 요금에 따라 3가지 등급으로 나눠주시고 (요금의 등급의 기준은 기초통계치 분위수 값으로 기준)\n",
        "    - 해당 분위수에 따라 남성과 여성을 추출하고 카운팅 수, 생존수 비교해 주세요.\n",
        "    \n",
        "- **필수과제3**  \n",
        "- 혼자온 사람과 혼자 오지 않은사람들 중에서 둘을 비교하는데\n",
        "    - 공통 조건은 혼자 온 사람의 성별 여부에 따른 전체 카운팅과 생존수 비교해 주세요!\n",
        "    \n",
        "    \n",
        "- 필수과제 요구조건\n",
        "    - 쥬피터노트북, 코드와 주석, 데이터 비교값을 공유"
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "import pandas as pd\n",
        "import seaborn as sns\n",
        "\n",
        "# 타이타닉 데이터셋 로드\n",
        "titanic = sns.load_dataset('titanic')\n",
        "\n",
        "# pclass가 3이고 나이가 20세 미만인 데이터 필터링\n",
        "filtered_data = titanic[(titanic['pclass'] == 3) & (titanic['age'] < 20)]\n",
        "\n",
        "# 남성(Male) 데이터와 여성(Female) 데이터 분리\n",
        "male_data = filtered_data[filtered_data['sex'] == 'male']\n",
        "female_data = filtered_data[filtered_data['sex'] == 'female']\n",
        "\n",
        "# 남성과 여성의 총 카운트\n",
        "male_count = len(male_data)\n",
        "female_count = len(female_data)\n",
        "\n",
        "# 남성과 여성의 생존자 수\n",
        "male_survived = male_data[male_data['survived'] == 1].shape[0]\n",
        "female_survived = female_data[female_data['survived'] == 1].shape[0]\n",
        "\n",
        "# 결과 출력\n",
        "print(f\"필수과제 1 - pclass 3, 나이 20세 미만 남성 카운트: {male_count}, 생존자: {male_survived}\")\n",
        "print(f\"필수과제 1 - pclass 3, 나이 20세 미만 여성 카운트: {female_count}, 생존자: {female_survived}\")"
      ],
      "metadata": {
        "id": "s2sMJ17GbQT2",
        "outputId": "8bdb7887-3119-4e10-e8c6-ffd742b2ba15",
        "colab": {
          "base_uri": "https://localhost:8080/"
        }
      },
      "id": "s2sMJ17GbQT2",
      "execution_count": 39,
      "outputs": [
        {
          "output_type": "stream",
          "name": "stdout",
          "text": [
            "필수과제 1 - pclass 3, 나이 20세 미만 남성 카운트: 63, 생존자: 12\n",
            "필수과제 1 - pclass 3, 나이 20세 미만 여성 카운트: 45, 생존자: 24\n"
          ]
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "# 요금의 분위수 계산 (1/3, 2/3 분위수 기준으로 요금을 나눔)\n",
        "fare_1_3, fare_2_3 = titanic['fare'].quantile([1/3, 2/3])\n",
        "\n",
        "# 요금 등급에 따른 조건\n",
        "low_fare = titanic[titanic['fare'] <= fare_1_3]\n",
        "mid_fare = titanic[(titanic['fare'] > fare_1_3) & (titanic['fare'] <= fare_2_3)]\n",
        "high_fare = titanic[titanic['fare'] > fare_2_3]\n",
        "\n",
        "# 각 요금 등급에서 남성과 여성의 생존자 수 및 전체 카운트 계산\n",
        "def count_gender_survival(data, label):\n",
        "    male_data = data[data['sex'] == 'male']\n",
        "    female_data = data[data['sex'] == 'female']\n",
        "    print(f\"{label} 등급 요금 - 남성: {len(male_data)}, 생존자: {male_data[male_data['survived'] == 1].shape[0]}\")\n",
        "    print(f\"{label} 등급 요금 - 여성: {len(female_data)}, 생존자: {female_data[female_data['survived'] == 1].shape[0]}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# 결과 출력\n",

        "# 혼자 온 사람과 혼자 오지 않은 사람 데이터 분리\n",
        "alone_data = titanic[titanic['alone'] == True]\n",
        "not_alone_data = titanic[titanic['alone'] == False]\n",
        "\n",
        "# 혼자 온 사람과 혼자 오지 않은 사람의 성별 카운트와 생존자 수 계산\n",
        "def count_alone_gender_survival(data, label):\n",
        "    male_data = data[data['sex'] == 'male']\n",
        "    female_data = data[data['sex'] == 'female']\n",
        "    print(f\"{label} - 남성: {len(male_data)}, 생존자: {male_data[male_data['survived'] == 1].shape[0]}\")\n",
        "    print(f\"{label} - 여성: {len(female_data)}, 생존자: {female_data[female_data['survived'] == 1].shape[0]}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# 결과 출력\n",

        "count_alone_gender_survival(alone_data, \"혼자 온 사람\")\n",
